            <span class="off-screen">Video</span>
            <h1 class="vxp-media__headline">The statue saving a coral reef in the Philippines</h1>
            <div class="vxp-media__summary"><p>Eight years ago a statue of the Virgin Mary was sunk off the coast of Bohol in the Philippines to try to stop dynamite fishing because it was destroying precious marine life.</p><p>Now the "Sea Knights" have returned to see if it has been a success.</p><p><i>Video Journalist: Howard Johnson</i></p><p><i>Producer: Virma Simonette</i></p><p><i>Additional footage: Tim Consul, Rodrick Francia and Rex Villavelez.</i></p></div>
                <ul class="vxp-media__info-list mini-info-list">
                    <li class="mini-info-list__item">
                        <div class="mini-info-list__date vxp-date" data-seconds="1521509133" data-datetime="20 March 2018">20 Mar 2018</div>
                    </li>
                </ul>

                                istats.log('error', 'orb-footer-promo-failed');
                                bbccookies.set('ckns_orb_nopromo=1; expires=' + new Date(new Date().getTime() + 1000 * 60 * 10).toGMTString() + ';path=/;');
                             }
                        });   
                    }
                });
            }
        }
    };
    
        
    define('orb/promomanager', ['orb/lib/_event'], function (event) {
        event.mixin(promoManager);
        return promoManager;
    });
    
    require(['orb/promomanager'], function (promoManager) {
        promoManager.init(document.getElementById('navp-orb-footer-promo'));
    })
})();
